23→\t\"time\"\n    24→\n    25→\tdiscovery \"github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/service/discovery/v3\"\n    26→\t\"github.com/google/uuid\"\n    27→\t\"go.uber.org/atomic\"\n    28→\t\"golang.org/x/time/rate\"\n    29→\t\"google.golang.org/grpc\"\n    30→\n    31→\t\"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/autoregistration\"\n    32→\t\"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/features\"\n    33→\t\"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/model\"\n    34→\t\"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/networking/core/envoyfilter\"\n    35→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/cluster\"\n    36→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config/schema/kind\"\n    37→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/kube/krt\"\n    38→\tistiolog \"istio.io/istio/pkg/log\"\n    39→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/maps\"\n  47→\t// DebounceAfter is the delay added to events to wait\n    48→\t// after a registry/config event for debouncing.\n    49→\t// This will delay the push by at least this interval, plus\n    50→\t// the time getting subsequent events. If no change is\n    51→\t// detected the push will happen, otherwise we'll keep\n    52→\t// delaying until things settle.\n    53→\tDebounceAfter time.Duration\n    54→\n    55→\t// debounceMax is the maximum time to wait for events\n    56→\t// while debouncing. Defaults to 10 seconds. If events keep\n    57→\t// showing up with no break for this time, we'll trigger a push.\n    58→\tdebounceMax time.Duration\n    59→\n    60→\t// enableEDSDebounce indicates whether EDS pushes should be debounced.\n    61→\tenableEDSDebounce bool\n    62→}\n    63→\n    64→// DiscoveryServer is Pilot's gRPC implementation for Envoy's xds APIs\n    65→type DiscoveryServer struct {\n    66→\t// Env is the model environment.\n    67→\tEnv *model.Environment\n    68→\n    69→\t// Generators allow customizing the generated config, based on the client metadata.\n    70→\t// Key is the generator type - will match the Generator metadata to set the per-connection\n    71→\t// default generator, or the combination of Generator metadata and TypeUrl to select a\n    72→\t// different generator for a type.\n    73→\t// Normal istio clients use the default generator - will not be impacted by this.\n    74→\tGenerators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator\n    75→\n    76→\t// ProxyNeedsPush is a function that determines whether a push can be completely skipped. Individual generators\n    77→\t// may also choose to not send any updates.\n    78→\tProxyNeedsPush func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool)\n    79→\n    80→\t// concurrentPushLimit is a semaphore that limits the amount of concurrent XDS pushes.\n    81→\tconcurrentPushLimit chan struct{}\n    82→\t// RequestRateLimit limits the number of new XDS requests allowed. This helps prevent thundering hurd of incoming requests.\n    83→\tRequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter\n    84→\n    85→\t// InboundUpdates describes the number of configuration updates the discovery server has received\n    86→\tInboundUpdates *atomic.Int64\n    87→\t// CommittedUpdates describes the number of configuration updates the discovery server has\n    88→\t// received, process, and stored in the push context. If this number is less than InboundUpdates,\n    89→\t// there are updates we have not yet processed.\n    90→\t// Note: This does not mean that all proxies have received these configurations; it is strictly\n    91→\t// the push context, which means that the next push to a proxy will receive this configuration.\n    92→\tCommittedUpdates *atomic.Int64\n    93→\n    94→\t// pushChannel is the buffer used for debouncing.\n    95→\t// after debouncing the pushRequest will be sent to pushQueue\n    96→\tpushChannel chan *model.PushRequest\n    97→\n    98→\t// pushQueue is the buffer that used after debounce and before the real xds push.\n    99→\tpushQueue *PushQueue\n   100→\n   101→\t// debugHandlers is the list of all the supported debug handlers.\n   102→\tdebugHandlers map[string]string\n   103→\n   104→\t// adsClients reflect active gRPC channels, for both ADS and EDS.\n   105→\tadsClients      map[string]*Connection\n   106→\tadsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex\n   107→\n   108→\t// Authenticators for XDS requests. Should be same/subset of the CA authenticators.\n   109→\tAuthenticators []security.Authenticator\n   110→\n   111→\tWorkloadEntryController *autoregistration.Controller\n   112→\n   113→\t// serverReady indicates caches have been synced up and server is ready to process requests.\n   114→\tserverReady atomic.Bool\n   115→\n   116→\tDebounceOptions DebounceOptions\n   117→\n   118→\t// Cache for XDS resources\n   119→\tCache model.XdsCache\n   120→\n   121→\t// JwtKeyResolver holds a reference to the JWT key resolver instance.\n   122→\tJwtKeyResolver *model.JwksResolver\n   123→\n   124→\t// ListRemoteClusters collects debug information about other clusters this istiod reads from.\n   125→\tListRemoteClusters func() []cluster.DebugInfo\n   126→\n   127→\t// ClusterAliases are alias names for cluster. When a proxy connects with a cluster ID\n   128→\t// and if it has a different alias we should use that a cluster ID for proxy.\n   129→\tClusterAliases map[cluster.ID]cluster.ID\n   130→\n   131→\t// pushVersion stores the numeric push version. This should be accessed via NextVersion()\n   132→\tpushVersion atomic.Uint64\n   133→\n   134→\t// DiscoveryStartTime is the time since the binary started\n   135→\tDiscoveryStartTime time.Time\n   136→\n   137→\tkrtDebugger *krt.DebugHandler\n   138→}\n   139→\n   140→// NewDiscoveryServer creates DiscoveryServer that sources data from Pilot's internal mesh data structures\n   141→func NewDiscoveryServer(env *model.Environment, clusterAliases map[string]string, debugger *krt.DebugHandler) *DiscoveryServer {\n   142→\tout := &DiscoveryServer{\n   143→\t\tEnv:                 env,\n   144→\t\tGenerators:          map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator{},\n   145→\t\tProxyNeedsPush:      DefaultProxyNeedsPush,\n   146→\t\tconcurrentPushLimit: make(chan struct{}, features.PushThrottle),\n   147→\t\tRequestRateLimit:    rate.NewLimiter(rate.Limit(features.RequestLimit), 1),\n   148→\t\tInboundUpdates:      atomic.NewInt64(0),\n   149→\t\tCommittedUpdates:    atomic.NewInt64(0),\n   150→\t\tpushChannel:         make(chan *model.PushRequest, 10),\n   151→\t\tpushQueue:           NewPushQueue(),\n   152→\t\tdebugHandlers:       map[string]string{},\n   153→\t\tadsClients:          map[string]*Connection{},\n   154→\t\tkrtDebugger:         debugger,\n   155→\t\tDebounceOptions: DebounceOptions{\n   156→\t\t\tDebounceAfter:     features.DebounceAfter,\n   157→\t\t\tdebounceMax:       features.DebounceMax,\n   158→\t\t\tenableEDSDebounce: features.EnableEDSDebounce,\n   159→\t\t},\n   160→\t\tCache:              env.Cache,\n   161→\t\tDiscoveryStartTime: processStartTime,\n   162→\t}\n   163→\n   164→\tout.ClusterAliases = make(map[cluster.ID]cluster.ID)\n   165→\tfor alias := range clusterAliases {\n   166→\t\tout.ClusterAliases[cluster.ID(alias)] = cluster.ID(clusterAliases[alias])\n   167→\t}\n   168→\n   169→\tout.initJwksResolver()\n   170→\n   171→\treturn out\n   172→}\n   173→\n   174→// initJwkResolver initializes the JWT key resolver to be used.\n   175→func (s *DiscoveryServer) initJwksResolver() {\n   176→\tif s.JwtKeyResolver != nil {\n   177→\t\ts.closeJwksResolver()\n   178→\t}\n   179→\ts.JwtKeyResolver = model.NewJwksResolver(\n   180→\t\tmodel.JwtPubKeyEvictionDuration, model.JwtPubKeyRefreshInterval,\n   181→\t\tmodel.JwtPubKeyRefreshIntervalOnFailure, model.JwtPubKeyRetryInterval)\n   182→\n   183→\t// Flush cached discovery responses when detecting jwt public key change.\n   184→\ts.JwtKeyResolver.PushFunc = func() {\n   185→\t\ts.ConfigUpdate(&model.PushRequest{Full: true, Reason: model.NewReasonStats(model.UnknownTrigger), Forced: true})\n   186→\t}\n   187→}\n   188→\n   189→// closeJwksResolver shuts down the JWT key resolver used.\n   190→func (s *DiscoveryServer) closeJwksResolver() {\n   191→\tif s.JwtKeyResolver != nil {\n   192→\t\ts.JwtKeyResolver.Close()\n   193→\t}\n   194→}\n   195→\n   196→// Register adds the ADS handler to the grpc server\n   197→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Register(rpcs *grpc.Server) {\n   198→\t// Register v3 server\n   199→\tdiscovery.RegisterAggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer(rpcs, s)\n   200→}\n   201→\n   202→var processStartTime = time.Now()\n   203→\n   204→// CachesSynced is called when caches have been synced so that server can accept connections.\n   205→func (s *DiscoveryServer) CachesSynced() {\n   206→\tlog.Infof(\"All caches have been synced up in %v, marking server ready\", time.Since(s.DiscoveryStartTime))\n   207→\ts.serverReady.Store(true)\n   208→}\n   209→\n   210→func (s *DiscoveryServer) IsServerReady() bool {\n   211→\treturn s.serverReady.Load()\n   212→}\n   213→\n   214→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Start(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   215→\tgo s.WorkloadEntryController.Run(stopCh)\n   216→\tgo s.handleUpdates(stopCh)\n   217→\tgo s.periodicRefreshMetrics(stopCh)\n   218→\tgo s.sendPushes(stopCh)\n   219→\tgo s.Cache.Run(stopCh)\n   220→}\n   221→\n   222→// Push metrics are updated periodically (10s default)\n   223→func (s *DiscoveryServer) periodicRefreshMetrics(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   224→\tticker := time.NewTicker(periodicRefreshMetrics)\n   225→\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n   226→\tfor {\n   227→\t\tselect {\n   228→\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n   229→\t\t\tpush := s.globalPushContext()\n   230→\t\t\tmodel.LastPushMutex.Lock()\n   231→\t\t\tif model.LastPushStatus != push {\n   232→\t\t\t\tmodel.LastPushStatus = push\n   233→\t\t\t\tpush.UpdateMetrics()\n   234→\t\t\t\tout, _ := model.LastPushStatus.StatusJSON()\n   235→\t\t\t\tif string(out) != \"{}\" {\n   236→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push Status: %s\", string(out))\n   237→\t\t\t\t}\n   238→\t\t\t}\n   239→\t\t\tmodel.LastPushMutex.Unlock()\n   240→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   241→\t\t\treturn\n   242→\t\t}\n   243→\t}\n   244→}\n   245→\n   246→// dropCacheForRequest clears the cache in response to a push request\n   247→func (s *DiscoveryServer) dropCacheForRequest(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   248→\t// If we don't know what updated, cannot safely cache. Clear the whole cache\n   249→\tif req.Forced {\n   250→\t\ts.Cache.ClearAll()\n   251→\t} else {\n   252→\t\t// Otherwise, just clear the updated configs\n   253→\t\ts.Cache.Clear(req.ConfigsUpdated)\n   254→\t}\n   255→}\n   256→\n   257→// Push is called to push changes on config updates using ADS.\n   258→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Push(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   259→\tif !req.Full {\n   260→\t\treq.Push = s.globalPushContext()\n   261→\t\ts.dropCacheForRequest(req)\n   262→\t\ts.AdsPushAll(req)\n   263→\t\treturn\n   264→\t}\n   265→\t// Reset the status during the push.\n   266→\toldPushContext := s.globalPushContext()\n   267→\tif oldPushContext != nil {\n   268→\t\toldPushContext.OnConfigChange()\n   269→\t\t// Push the previous push Envoy metrics.\n   270→\t\tenvoyfilter.RecordMetrics()\n   271→\t}\n   272→\t// PushContext is reset after a config change. Previous status is\n   273→\t// saved.\n   274→\tt0 := time.Now()\n   275→\tversionLocal := s.NextVersion()\n   276→\tpush := s.initPushContext(req, oldPushContext, versionLocal)\n   277→\tinitContextTime := time.Since(t0)\n   278→\tlog.Debugf(\"InitContext %v for push took %s\", versionLocal, initContextTime)\n   279→\tpushContextInitTime.Record(initContextTime.Seconds())\n   280→\n   281→\treq.Push = push\n   282→\ts.AdsPushAll(req)\n   283→}\n   284→\n   285→func nonce(noncePrefix string) string {\n   286→\treturn noncePrefix + uuid.New().String()\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// Returns the global push context. This should be used with caution; generally the proxy-specific\n   290→// PushContext should be used to get the current state in the context of a single proxy. This should\n   291→// only be used for \"global\" lookups, such as initiating a new push to all proxies.\n   292→func (s *DiscoveryServer) globalPushContext() *model.PushContext {\n   293→\treturn s.Env.PushContext()\n   294→}\n   295→\n   296→var fullPushLog = istiolog.RegisterScope(\"fullpush\", \"logs details about why Istio is triggering a full push\")\n   297→\n   298→// ConfigUpdate implements ConfigUpdater interface, used to request pushes.\n   299→func (s *DiscoveryServer) ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   300→\tif features.EnableUnsafeAssertions {\n   301→\t\tif model.HasConfigsOfKind(req.ConfigsUpdated, kind.Service) {\n   302→\t\t\tpanic(\"assertion failed kind.Service can not be set in ConfigKey\")\n   303→\t\t}\n   304→\t}\n   305→\tif model.HasConfigsOfKind(req.ConfigsUpdated, kind.Address) {\n   306→\t\t// This is a bit like clearing EDS cache on EndpointShard update. Because Address\n   307→\t\t// types are fetched dynamically, they are not part of the same protections, so we need to clear\n   308→\t\t// the cache.\n   309→\t\ts.Cache.ClearAll()\n   310→\t}\n   311→\tinboundConfigUpdates.Increment()\n   312→\ts.InboundUpdates.Inc()\n   313→\tif req.Full && fullPushLog.DebugEnabled() {\n   314→\t\tconfigs := slices.Sort(slices.Map(req.ConfigsUpdated.UnsortedList(), model.ConfigKey.String))\n   315→\t\treasons := maps.Keys(req.Reason)\n   316→\t\tfullPushLog.Debugf(\"full push triggered configs=%v reasons=%v\", configs, reasons)\n   317→\t}\n   318→\ts.pushChannel <- req\n   319→}\n   320→\n   321→// Debouncing and push request happens in a separate thread, it uses locks\n   322→// and we want to avoid complications, ConfigUpdate may already hold other locks.\n   323→// handleUpdates processes events from pushChannel\n   324→// It ensures that at minimum minQuiet time has elapsed since the last event before processing it.\n   325→// It also ensures that at most maxDelay is elapsed between receiving an event and processing it.\n   326→func (s *DiscoveryServer) handleUpdates(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   327→\tdebounce(s.pushChannel, stopCh, s.DebounceOptions, s.Push, s.CommittedUpdates)\n   328→}\n   329→\n   330→// The debounce helper function is implemented to enable mocking\n   331→func debounce(ch chan *model.PushRequest, stopCh <-chan struct{}, opts DebounceOptions, pushFn func(req *model.PushRequest), updateSent *atomic.Int64) {\n   332→\tvar timeChan <-chan time.Time\n   333→\tvar startDebounce time.Time\n   334→\tvar lastConfigUpdateTime time.Time\n   335→\n   336→\tpushCounter := 0\n   337→\tdebouncedEvents := 0\n   338→\n   339→\t// Keeps track of the push requests. If updates are debounce they will be merged.\n   340→\tvar req *model.PushRequest\n   341→\n   342→\tfree := true\n   343→\tfreeCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)\n   344→\n   345→\tpush := func(req *model.PushRequest, debouncedEvents int, startDebounce time.Time) {\n   346→\t\tpushFn(req)\n   347→\t\tupdateSent.Add(int64(debouncedEvents))\n   348→\t\tdebounceTime.Record(time.Since(startDebounce).Seconds())\n   349→\t\tfreeCh <- struct{}{}\n   350→\t}\n   351→\n   352→\tpushWorker := func() {\n   353→\t\teventDelay := time.Since(startDebounce)\n   354→\t\tquietTime := time.Since(lastConfigUpdateTime)\n   355→\t\t// it has been too long or quiet enough\n   356→\t\tif eventDelay >= opts.debounceMax || quietTime >= opts.DebounceAfter {\n   357→\t\t\tif req != nil {\n   358→\t\t\t\tpushCounter++\n   359→\t\t\t\tif req.ConfigsUpdated == nil {\n   360→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push debounce stable[%d] %d for reason %s: %v since last change, %v since last push, full=%v\",\n   361→\t\t\t\t\t\tpushCounter, debouncedEvents, reasonsUpdated(req),\n   362→\t\t\t\t\t\tquietTime, eventDelay, req.Full)\n   363→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   364→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Push debounce stable[%d] %d for config %s: %v since last change, %v since last push, full=%v\",\n   365→\t\t\t\t\t\tpushCounter, debouncedEvents, configsUpdated(req),\n   366→\t\t\t\t\t\tquietTime, eventDelay, req.Full)\n   367→\t\t\t\t}\n   368→\t\t\t\tfree = false\n   369→\t\t\t\tgo push(req, debouncedEvents, startDebounce)\n   370→\t\t\t\treq = nil\n   371→\t\t\t\tdebouncedEvents = 0\n   372→\t\t\t}\n   373→\t\t} else {\n   374→\t\t\ttimeChan = time.After(opts.DebounceAfter - quietTime)\n   375→\t\t}\n   376→\t}\n   377→\n   378→\tfor {\n   379→\t\tselect {\n   380→\t\tcase <-freeCh:\n   381→\t\t\tfree = true\n   382→\t\t\tpushWorker()\n   383→\t\tcase r := <-ch:\n   384→\t\t\t// If reason is not set, record it as an unknown reason\n   385→\t\t\tif len(r.Reason) == 0 {\n   386→\t\t\t\tr.Reason = model.NewReasonStats(model.UnknownTrigger)\n   387→\t\t\t}\n   388→\t\t\tif !opts.enableEDSDebounce && !r.Full {\n   389→\t\t\t\t// trigger push now, just for EDS\n   390→\t\t\t\tgo func(req *model.PushRequest) {\n   391→\t\t\t\t\tpushFn(req)\n   392→\t\t\t\t\tupdateSent.Inc()\n   393→\t\t\t\t}(r)\n   394→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   395→\t\t\t}\n   396→\n   397→\t\t\tlastConfigUpdateTime = time.Now()\n   398→\t\t\tif debouncedEvents == 0 {\n   399→\t\t\t\ttimeChan = time.After(opts.DebounceAfter)\n   400→\t\t\t\tstartDebounce = lastConfigUpdateTime\n   401→\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\tdebouncedEvents++\n   403→\n   404→\t\t\treq = req.Merge(r)\n   405→\t\tcase <-timeChan:\n   406→\t\t\tif free {\n   407→\t\t\t\tpushWorker()\n   408→\t\t\t}\n   409→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   410→\t\t\treturn\n   411→\t\t}\n   412→\t}\n   413→}\n   414→\n   415→func configsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n   416→\tconfigs := \"\"\n   417→\tfor key := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n   418→\t\tconfigs += key.String()\n   419→\t\tbreak\n   420→\t}\n   421→\tif len(req.ConfigsUpdated) > 1 {\n   422→\t\tmore := \" and \" + strconv.Itoa(len(req.ConfigsUpdated)-1) + \" more configs\"\n   423→\t\tconfigs += more\n   424→\t}\n   425→\treturn configs\n   426→}\n   427→\n   428→func reasonsUpdated(req *model.PushRequest) string {\n   429→\tvar (\n   430→\t\treason0, reason1            model.TriggerReason\n   431→\t\treason0Cnt, reason1Cnt, idx int\n   432→\t)\n   433→\tfor r, cnt := range req.Reason {\n   434→\t\tif idx == 0 {\n   435→\t\t\treason0, reason0Cnt = r, cnt\n   436→\t\t} else if idx == 1 {\n   437→\t\t\treason1, reason1Cnt = r, cnt\n   438→\t\t} else {\n   439→\t\t\tbreak\n   440→\t\t}\n   441→\t\tidx++\n   442→\t}\n   443→\n   444→\tswitch len(req.Reason) {\n   445→\tcase 0:\n   446→\t\treturn \"unknown\"\n   447→\tcase 1:\n   448→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt)\n   449→\tcase 2:\n   450→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d and %s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt, reason1, reason1Cnt)\n   451→\tdefault:\n   452→\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d and %d(%d) more reasons\", reason0, reason0Cnt, len(req.Reason)-1,\n   453→\t\t\treq.Reason.Count()-reason0Cnt)\n   454→\t}\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→func doSendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}, semaphore chan struct{}, queue *PushQueue) {\n   458→\tfor {\n   459→\t\tselect {\n   460→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   461→\t\t\treturn\n   462→\t\tdefault:\n   463→\t\t\t// We can send to it until it is full, then it will block until a pushes finishes and reads from it.\n   464→\t\t\t// This limits the number of pushes that can happen concurrently\n   465→\t\t\tsemaphore <- struct{}{}\n   466→\n   467→\t\t\t// Get the next proxy to push. This will block if there are no updates required.\n   468→\t\t\tclient, push, shuttingdown := queue.Dequeue()\n   469→\t\t\tif shuttingdown {\n   470→\t\t\t\treturn\n   471→\t\t\t}\n   472→\t\t\trecordPushTriggers(push.Reason)\n   473→\t\t\t// Signals that a push is done by reading from the semaphore, allowing another send on it.\n   474→\t\t\tdoneFunc := func() {\n   475→\t\t\t\tqueue.MarkDone(client)\n   476→\t\t\t\t<-semaphore\n   477→\t\t\t}\n   478→\n   479→\t\t\tproxiesQueueTime.Record(time.Since(push.Start).Seconds())\n   480→\t\t\tvar closed <-chan struct{}\n   481→\t\t\tif client.deltaStream != nil {\n   482→\t\t\t\tclosed = client.deltaStream.Context().Done()\n   483→\t\t\t} else {\n   484→\t\t\t\tclosed = client.StreamDone()\n   485→\t\t\t}\n   486→\t\t\tgo func() {\n   487→\t\t\t\tpushEv := &Event{\n   488→\t\t\t\t\tpushRequest: push,\n   489→\t\t\t\t\tdone:        doneFunc,\n   490→\t\t\t\t}\n   491→\n   492→\t\t\t\tselect {\n   493→\t\t\t\tcase client.PushCh() <- pushEv:\n   494→\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   495→\t\t\t\tcase <-closed: // grpc stream was closed\n   496→\t\t\t\t\tdoneFunc()\n   497→\t\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Client closed connection %v\", client.ID())\n   498→\t\t\t\t}\n   499→\t\t\t}()\n   500→\t\t}\n   501→\t}\n   502→}\n   503→\n   504→// initPushContext creates a global push context and stores it on the environment. reason1Cnt, idx int\n\t)\n\tfor r, cnt := range req.Reason {\n\t\tif idx == 0 {\n\t\t\treason0, reason0Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else if idx == 1 {\n\t\t\treason1, reason1Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else <-stopCh:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// We can send to it until it is full, then it will block until a pushes finishes and reads from it.\n\t\t\t// This limits the number of pushes that can Note: while this\n// method is technically thread safe (there are no data races), it should not be called in parallel;\n// if it is, then we may start two push context creations (say A, and B), but then write them in\n// reverse order, leaving us with a final version of A, which may be incomplete.\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initPushContext(req *model.PushRequest, oldPushContext *model.PushContext, version string) *model.PushContext {\n\tpush := model.NewPushContext()\n\tpush.PushVersion = version\n\tpush.JwtKeyResolver = s.JwtKeyResolver\n\tpush.InitContext(s.Env, oldPushContext, req)\n\n\ts.dropCacheForRequest(req)\n\ts.Env.SetPushContext(push)\n\n\treturn push\n}\n\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) sendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n\tdoSendPushes(stopCh, s.concurrentPushLimit, s.pushQueue)\n}\n\n// Shutdown shuts down DiscoveryServer components.\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Shutdown() {\n\ts.closeJwksResolver()\n\ts.pushQueue.ShutDown()\n}\n\n// Clients returns all currently connected clients. This method can be safely called concurrently,\n// but care should be taken with the underlying objects (ie model.Proxy) to ensure proper locking.\n// This method returns only fully initialized connections; for all connections, use AllClients\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Clients() []*Connection {\n\ts.adsClientsMutex.RLock()\n\tdefer s.adsClientsMutex.RUnlock()\n\tclients := make([]*Connection, 0, len(s.adsClients))\n\tfor _, con := range s.adsClients {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-con.InitializedCh():\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// Initialization not complete, skip\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tclients = append(clients, con)\n\t}\n\treturn clients\n}\n\n// SortedClients returns all currently connected clients in an ordered manner.\n// Sorting order priority is as follows: ClusterID, Namespace, ID.\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) SortedClients() []*Connection {\n\tclients := s.Clients()\n\tsort.Slice(clients, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\tif clients[i].proxy.GetClusterID().String() < clients[j].proxy.GetClusterID().String() {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\tif clients[i].proxy.GetNamespace() < clients[j].proxy.GetNamespace() {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn clients[i].proxy.GetID() < clients[j].proxy.GetID()\n\t})\n\treturn clients\n}\n\n// AllClients returns all connected clients, per Clients, but additionally includes uninitialized connections\n// Warning: callers must take care not to rely on the con.proxy field being set\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AllClients() []*Connection {\n\ts.adsClientsMutex.RLock()\n\tdefer s.adsClientsMutex.RUnlock()\n\treturn maps.Values(s.adsClients)\n}\n\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) WaitForRequestLimit(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tif s.RequestRateLimit.Limit() == 0 {\n\t\t// Allow opt out when rate limiting is set to 0qps\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\t// Give a bit of time for queue to clear out, but if not fail fast. reason1Cnt, idx int\n\t)\n\tfor r, cnt := range req.Reason {\n\t\tif idx == 0 {\n\t\t\treason0, reason0Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else if idx == 1 {\n\t\t\treason1, reason1Cnt = r, cnt\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tidx++\n\t}\n\n\tswitch len(req.Reason) {\n\tcase 0:\n\t\treturn \"unknown\"\n\tcase 1:\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:%d\", reason0, reason0Cnt)\n\tcase 2:\n\t\treturn len(req.Reason)-1,\n\t\t\treq.Reason.Count()-reason0Cnt)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc doSendPushes(stopCh <-chan struct{}, semaphore chan struct{}, queue *PushQueue) {\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// We can send to it until it is full, then it will block until a pushes finishes and reads from it.\n\t\t\t// This limits the number of pushes that can happen concurrently\n\t\t\tsemaphore <- struct{}{}\n\n\t\t\t// Get the next proxy to push. do cleanups\nfunc (s *Server) waitForShutdown(stop <-chan struct{}) {\n\tgo func() {\n\t\t<-stop\n\t\tclose(s.internalStop)\n\t\t_ = s.fileWatcher.Close()\n\n\t\tif s.cacertsWatcher != nil {\n\t\t\t_ = s.cacertsWatcher.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Stop gRPC services.  If gRPC services fail to stop in the shutdown duration,\n\t\t// force stop them. This does not happen normally.\n\t\tstopped := make(chan struct{})\n\t\tgo func() {\n\t\t\t// Some grpcServer implementations do not support GracefulStop. Unfortunately, this is not\n\t\t\t// exposed; they just panic. To avoid this, we will recover and do a standard Stop when its not\n\t\t\t// support.\n\t\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\t\tif r := recover(); r != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.grpcServer.Stop()\n\t\t\t\t\tif s.secureGrpcServer != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\ts.secureGrpcServer.Stop()\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tclose(stopped)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}()\n\t\t\ts.grpcServer.GracefulStop()\n\t\t\tif s.secureGrpcServer != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.secureGrpcServer.GracefulStop()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tclose(stopped)\n\t\t}()\n\n\t\tt := time.NewTimer(s.shutdownDuration)\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-t.C:\n\t\t\ts.grpcServer.Stop()\n\t\t\tif s.secureGrpcServer != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.secureGrpcServer.Stop()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase <-stopped:\n\t\t\tt.Stop()\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Stop HTTP services.\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), s.shutdownDuration)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t\tif err := s.httpServer.Shutdown(ctx); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Warn(err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif s.httpsServer != nil {\n\t\t\tif err := s.httpsServer.Shutdown(ctx); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Warn(err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Shutdown the DiscoveryServer.\n\t\ts.XDSServer.Shutdown()\n\t}()\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) initGrpcServer(options *istiokeepalive.Options) {\n\tinterceptors := []grpc.UnaryServerInterceptor{\n\t\t// setup server prometheus monitoring (as final interceptor in chain)\n\t\tgrpcprom.UnaryServerInterceptor,\n\t}\n\tgrpcOptions := istiogrpc.ServerOptions(options, xdspkg.RecordRecvSize, interceptors...)\n\ts.grpcServer = grpc.NewServer(grpcOptions...)\n\ts.XDSServer.Register(s.grpcServer)\n\treflection.Register(s.grpcServer)\n}\n\n// initialize secureGRPCServer.\nfunc (s *Server) initSecureDiscoveryService(args *PilotArgs, trustDomain string) error {\n\tif args.ServerOptions.SecureGRPCAddr == \"\" {\n\t\tlog.Info(\"The secure discovery port is disabled, multiplexing on httpAddr \")\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tpeerCertVerifier, err := s.createPeerCertVerifier(args.ServerOptions.TLSOptions, trustDomain)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tif peerCertVerifier == nil {\n\t\t// Running locally without configured certs - no TLS mode\n\t\tlog.Warnf(\"The secure discovery service is disabled\")\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tlog.Info(\"initializing secure discovery service\")\n\n\tcfg := &tls.Config{\n\t\tGetCertificate: s.getIstiodCertificate,\n\t\tClientAuth:     tls.VerifyClientCertIfGiven,\n\t\tClientCAs:      peerCertVerifier.GetGeneralCertPool(),\n\t\tVerifyPeerCertificate: func(rawCerts [][]byte, verifiedChains [][]*x509.Certificate) error {\n\t\t\terr := peerCertVerifier.VerifyPeerCert(rawCerts, verifiedChains)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Infof(\"Could not verify certificate: %v\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t},\n\t\tMinVersion:   tls.VersionTLS12,\n\t\tCipherSuites: args.ServerOptions.TLSOptions.CipherSuites,\n\t}\n\t// Compliance for xDS server TLS.\n\tsec_model.EnforceGoCompliance(cfg)\n\n\ttlsCreds := credentials.NewTLS(cfg)\n\n\ts.secureGrpcAddress = args.ServerOptions.SecureGRPCAddr\n\n\tinterceptors := []grpc.UnaryServerInterceptor{\n\t\t// setup server prometheus monitoring (as final interceptor in chain)\n\t\tgrpcprom.UnaryServerInterceptor,\n\t}\n\topts := istiogrpc.ServerOptions(args.KeepaliveOptions, xdspkg.RecordRecvSize, interceptors...)\n\topts = append(opts, grpc.Creds(tlsCreds))\n\n\ts.secureGrpcServer = grpc.NewServer(opts...)\n\ts.XDSServer.Register(s.secureGrpcServer)\n\treflection.Register(s.secureGrpcServer)\n\n\ts.addStartFunc(\"secure gRPC\", func(stop <-chan struct{}) error {\n\t\tgo func() {\n\t\t\t<-stop\n\t\t\ts.secureGrpcServer.Stop()\n\t\t}()\n\t\treturn nil\n\t})\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// addStartFunc appends a function to be run. These are run synchronously in order,\n// so the function should start a go routine if it needs to do anything blocking\nfunc (s *Server) addStartFunc(name string, fn server.Component) {\n\ts.server.RunComponent(name, fn)\n}\n\n// adds a readiness probe for Istiod Server.\nfunc (s *Server) addReadinessProbe(name string, fn readinessProbe) {\n\ts.readinessProbes[name] = fn\n}\n\n// addTerminatingStartFunc adds a function that should terminate before the serve shuts down\n// This is useful to do cleanup activities\n// This is does not guarantee they will terminate gracefully - best effort only\n// Function should be synchronous; once it returns it is considered \"done\"\nfunc (s *Server) addTerminatingStartFunc(name string, fn server.Component) {\n\ts.server.RunComponentAsyncAndWait(name, fn)\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) waitForCacheSync(stop <-chan struct{}) bool {\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\tlog.Info(\"Waiting for caches to be synced\")\n\tif !kubelib.WaitForCacheSync(\"server\", stop, s.cachesSynced) {\n\t\tlog.Errorf(\"Failed waiting for cache sync\")\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tlog.Infof(\"All controller caches have been synced up in %v\", time.Since(start))\n\n\t// At this point, we know that all update events of the initial state-of-the-world have been\n\t// received. We wait to ensure we have committed at least this many updates. This avoids a race\n\t// condition where we are marked ready prior to updating the push context, leading to incomplete\n\t// pushes.\n\texpected := s.XDSServer.InboundUpdates.Load()\n\treturn kubelib.WaitForCacheSync(\"push context\", stop, func() bool { return s.pushContextReady(expected) })\n}\n\n// pushContextReady indicates whether pushcontext has processed all inbound config updates.\nfunc (s *Server) pushContextReady(expected int64) bool {\n\tcommitted := s.XDSServer.CommittedUpdates.Load()\n\tif committed < expected {\n\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Waiting for pushcontext to process inbound updates, inbound: %v, committed : %v\", expected, committed)\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// cachesSynced checks whether caches have been synced.\nfunc (s *Server) cachesSynced() bool {\n\tif s.multiclusterController != nil && !s.multiclusterController.HasSynced() {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tif !s.ServiceController().HasSynced() {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tif !s.configController.HasSynced() {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// initRegistryEventHandlers sets up event handlers for config and service updates\nfunc (s *Server) initRegistryEventHandlers() {\n\tlog.Info(\"initializing registry event handlers\")\n\t// Flush cached discovery responses whenever services configuration change.\n\tserviceHandler := func(prev, curr *model.Service, event model.Event) {\n\t\tpushReq := &model.PushRequest{\n\t\t\tFull:           true,\n\t\t\tConfigsUpdated: sets.New(model.ConfigKey{Kind: kind.ServiceEntry, Name: string(curr.Hostname), Namespace: curr.Attributes.Namespace}),\n\t\t\tReason:         model.NewReasonStats(model.ServiceUpdate),\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.XDSServer.ConfigUpdate(pushReq)\n\t}\n\ts.ServiceController().AppendServiceHandler(serviceHandler)\n\n\tif s.configController != nil {\n\t\tconfigHandler := func(prev config.Config, curr config.Config, event model.Event) {\n\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Handle event %s for configuration %s\", event, curr.Key())\n\t\t\t// For update events, trigger push only if spec has changed.\n\t\t\tif event == model.EventUpdate && !needsPush(prev, curr) {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"skipping push for %s as spec has not changed\", prev.Key())\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpushReq := &model.PushRequest{\n\t\t\t\tFull:           true,\n\t\t\t\tConfigsUpdated: sets.New(model.ConfigKey{Kind: gvk.MustToKind(curr.GroupVersionKind), Name: curr.Name, Namespace: curr.Namespace}),\n\t\t\t\tReason:         model.NewReasonStats(model.ConfigUpdate),\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\ts.XDSServer.ConfigUpdate(pushReq)\n\t\t}\n\t\tschemas := collections.Pilot.All()\n\t\tif features.EnableGatewayAPI {\n\t\t\tschemas = collections.PilotGatewayAPI().All()\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, schema := range schemas {\n\t\t\t// This resource type was handled in external/servicediscovery.go, no need to rehandle here.\n\t\t\tif schema.GroupVersionKind() == gvk.ServiceEntry {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif schema.GroupVersionKind() == gvk.WorkloadEntry {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif schema.GroupVersionKind() == gvk.WorkloadGroup {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Already handled by gateway controller\n\t\t\tif schema.GroupVersionKind().Group == gvk.KubernetesGateway.Group {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\ts.configController.RegisterEventHandler(schema.GroupVersionKind(), configHandler)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// initIstiodCertLoader will make sure istiodCertBundleWatcher is updating\n// the certs and updates Server.istiodCert - which is returned on all TLS requests.\nfunc (s *Server) initIstiodCertLoader() error {\n\tif err := s.loadIstiodCert(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"first time load IstiodCert failed: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\t_, watchCh := s.istiodCertBundleWatcher.AddWatcher()\n\ts.addStartFunc(\"reload certs\", func(stop <-chan struct{}) error {\n\t\tgo s.reloadIstiodCert(watchCh, stop)\n\t\treturn nil\n\t})\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// initIstiodCerts creates Istiod certificates to be used by gRPC and webhook TLS servers\n// and also sets up watches to them. It also detects and sets the root certificates\n// for replication.\n//\n// This will also detect the root CAs (mesh trust) and set it up for Istiod as well as\n// namespace replication, if the controller is enabled.\n//\n// Will prefer local certificates, and fallback to using the CA to sign a fresh, temporary\n// certificate.\nfunc (s *Server) initIstiodCerts(args *PilotArgs, host string) error {\n\t// Skip all certificates\n\tvar err error\n\n\ts.dnsNames = getDNSNames(args, host)\n\tif hasCustomCertArgsOrWellKnown, tlsCertPath, tlsKeyPath, caCertPath := hasCustomTLSCerts(args.ServerOptions.TLSOptions); hasCustomCertArgsOrWellKnown {\n\t\t// Use the DNS certificate provided via args or in well known location.\n\t\terr = s.initFileCertificateWatches(TLSOptions{\n\t\t\tCaCertFile: caCertPath,\n\t\t\tKeyFile:    tlsKeyPath,\n\t\t\tCertFile:   tlsCertPath,\n\t\t})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Not crashing istiod - This typically happens if certs are missing and in tests.\n\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"error initializing certificate watches: %v\", err)\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t} else if features.EnableCAServer && features.PilotCertProvider == constants.CertProviderIstiod {\n\t\tlog.Infof(\"initializing Istiod DNS certificates host: %s, custom host: %s\", host, features.IstiodServiceCustomHost)\n\t\terr = s.initDNSCertsIstiod()\n\t} else if features.PilotCertProvider == constants.CertProviderKubernetes {\n\t\t// This will not work - better to fail Istiod startup so it can be detected early.\n\t\t// Unlike other failures that we can recover from, this has no mitigation, user must\n\t\t// choose a different source.\n\t\t// The feature didn't work for few releases, but a skip-version upgrade may still\n\t\t// encounter it.\n\t\tlog.Fatal(\"PILOT_CERT_PROVIDER=kubernetes is no longer supported by upstream K8S\")\n\t} else if strings.HasPrefix(features.PilotCertProvider, constants.CertProviderKubernetesSignerPrefix) {\n\t\tlog.Infof(\"initializing Istiod DNS certificates using K8S RA:%s  host: %s, custom host: %s\", features.PilotCertProvider,\n\t\t\thost, features.IstiodServiceCustomHost)\n\t\terr = s.initDNSCertsK8SRA()\n\t} else {\n\t\tlog.Warnf(\"PILOT_CERT_PROVIDER=%s is not implemented\", features.PilotCertProvider)\n\n\t\t// In Istio 1.22 - we return nil here - the old code in s.initDNSCerts used to have\n\t\t// an 'else' to handle the unknown providers by not initializing the TLS certs but\n\t\t// still setting the root from /etc/certs/root-cert.pem for distribution in the\n\t\t// namespace controller.\n\t\t// The new behavior appears safer - IMO we may also do a fatal unless provider is\n\t\t// set to \"none\" because it is not clear what the user intends.\n\n\t\t// Skip invoking initIstiodCertLoader - we have no cert.\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\terr = s.initIstiodCertLoader()\n\t}\n\n\treturn err\n}\n\nfunc getDNSNames(args *PilotArgs, host string) []string {\n\t// Append custom hostname if there is any\n\tcustomHost := features.IstiodServiceCustomHost\n\tvar cHosts []string\n\n\tif customHost != \"\" {\n\t\tcHosts = strings.Split(customHost, \",\")\n\t}\n\tsans := sets.New(cHosts...)\n\tsans.Insert(host)\n\t// The first is the recommended one, also used by Apiserver for webhooks.\n\t// add a few known hostnames\n\tknownHosts := []string{\"istiod\", \"istiod-remote\", \"istio-pilot\"}\n\t// In some conditions, pilot address for sds is different from other xds,\n\t// like multi-cluster primary-remote mode with revision.\n\tif args.Revision != \"\" && args.Revision != \"default\" {\n\t\tknownHosts = append(knownHosts, \"istiod\"+\"-\"+args.Revision)\n\t}\n\tknownSans := make([]string, 0, 2*len(knownHosts))\n\tfor _, altName := range knownHosts {\n\t\tknownSans = append(knownSans,\n\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s.%s.svc\", altName, args.Namespace))\n\t}\n\tsans.InsertAll(knownSans...)\n\tdnsNames := sets.SortedList(sans)\n\tlog.Infof(\"Discover server subject alt names: %v\", dnsNames)\n\treturn dnsNames\n}\n\n// createPeerCertVerifier creates a SPIFFE certificate verifier with the current istiod configuration.\nfunc (s *Server) createPeerCertVerifier(tlsOptions TLSOptions, trustDomain string) (*spiffe.PeerCertVerifier, error) {\n\tcustomTLSCertsExists, _, _, caCertPath := hasCustomTLSCerts(tlsOptions)\n\tif !customTLSCertsExists && s.CA == nil && !s.isK8SSigning() {\n\t\t// Running locally without configured certs - no TLS mode\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\tpeerCertVerifier := spiffe.NewPeerCertVerifier()\n\tvar rootCertBytes []byte\n\tvar err error\n\tif caCertPath != \"\" {\n\t\tif rootCertBytes, err = os.ReadFile(caCertPath); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif s.RA != nil {\n\t\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(features.PilotCertProvider, constants.CertProviderKubernetesSignerPrefix) {\n\t\t\t\tsignerName := strings.TrimPrefix(features.PilotCertProvider, constants.CertProviderKubernetesSignerPrefix)\n\t\t\t\tcaBundle, _ := s.RA.GetRootCertFromMeshConfig(signerName)\n\t\t\t\trootCertBytes = append(rootCertBytes, caBundle...)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\trootCertBytes = append(rootCertBytes, s.RA.GetCAKeyCertBundle().GetRootCertPem()...)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif s.CA != nil {\n\t\t\trootCertBytes = append(rootCertBytes, s.CA.GetCAKeyCertBundle().GetRootCertPem()...)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(rootCertBytes) != 0 {\n\t\t// TODO: trustDomain here is static and will not update if it dynamically changes in mesh config\n\t\terr := peerCertVerifier.AddMappingFromPEM(trustDomain, rootCertBytes)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"add root CAs into peerCertVerifier failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn peerCertVerifier, nil\n}\n\nfunc checkPathsExist(paths ...string) bool {\n\tfor _, path := range paths {\n\t\tfInfo, err := os.Stat(path)\n\n\t\tif err != nil || fInfo.IsDir() {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// hasCustomTLSCerts returns the tls cert paths, used both if custom TLS certificates are configured via args or by mounting in well known.\n// while tls args should still take precedence the aim is to encourage loading the DNS tls cert in the well known path locations.\nfunc hasCustomTLSCerts(tlsOptions TLSOptions) (ok bool, tlsCertPath, tlsKeyPath, caCertPath string) {\n\t// load from tls args as priority\n\tif hasCustomTLSCertArgs(tlsOptions) {\n\t\treturn true, tlsOptions.CertFile, tlsOptions.KeyFile, tlsOptions.CaCertFile\n\t}\n\n\tif ok = checkPathsExist(constants.DefaultPilotTLSCert, constants.DefaultPilotTLSKey, constants.DefaultPilotTLSCaCert); ok {\n\t\ttlsCertPath = constants.DefaultPilotTLSCert\n\t\ttlsKeyPath = constants.DefaultPilotTLSKey\n\t\tcaCertPath = constants.DefaultPilotTLSCaCert\n\t\treturn ok, tlsCertPath, tlsKeyPath, caCertPath\n\t}\n\n\tif ok = checkPathsExist(constants.DefaultPilotTLSCert, constants.DefaultPilotTLSKey, constants.DefaultPilotTLSCaCertAlternatePath); ok {\n\t\ttlsCertPath = constants.DefaultPilotTLSCert\n\t\ttlsKeyPath = constants.DefaultPilotTLSKey\n\t\tcaCertPath = constants.DefaultPilotTLSCaCertAlternatePath\n\t\treturn ok, tlsCertPath, tlsKeyPath, caCertPath\n\t}\n\n\treturn ok, tlsCertPath, tlsKeyPath, caCertPath\n}\n\n// hasCustomTLSCerts returns true if custom TLS certificates are configured via args.\nfunc hasCustomTLSCertArgs(tlsOptions TLSOptions) bool {\n\treturn tlsOptions.CaCertFile != \"\" && tlsOptions.CertFile != \"\" && tlsOptions.KeyFile != \"\"\n}\n\n// getIstiodCertificate returns the istiod certificate, used in GetCertificate hook.\nfunc (s *Server) getIstiodCertificate(*tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Certificate, error) {\n\ts.certMu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.certMu.RUnlock()\n\tif s.istiodCert != nil {\n\t\treturn s.istiodCert, nil\n\t}\n\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cert not initialized\")\n}\n\n// initControllers initializes the controllers.\nfunc (s *Server) initControllers(args *PilotArgs) error {\n\tlog.Info(\"initializing controllers\")\n\ts.initMulticluster(args)\n\n\ts.initSDSServer()\n\n\tif features.EnableNodeUntaintControllers {\n\t\ts.initNodeUntaintController(args)\n\t}\n\n\tif features.EnableIPAutoallocate {\n\t\t// validate the IP autoallocate CIDR prefixes for IPv4 and IPv6\n\t\tif maybeCreateCA creates and initializes the built-in CA if needed.\nfunc (s *Server) maybeCreateCA(caOpts *caOptions) error {\n\t// CA signing certificate must be created only if CA is enabled.\n\tif features.EnableCAServer {\n\t\tlog.Info(\"creating CA and initializing public key\")\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif useRemoteCerts.Get() {\n\t\t\tif err = s.loadCACerts(caOpts, LocalCertDir.Get()); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to load remote CA certs: %v\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\t// May return nil, if the CA is missing required configs - This is not an error.\n\t\t// This is currently only used for K8S signing.\n\t\tif caOpts.ExternalCAType != \"\" {\n\t\t\tif s.RA, err = s.createIstioRA(caOpts); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create RA: %v\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\t// If K8S signs - we don't need to use the built-in istio CA.\n\t\tif !s.isK8SSigning() {\n\t\t\tif s.CA, err = s.createIstioCA(caOpts); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create CA: %v\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Returns true to indicate the K8S multicluster controller should enable replication of\n// root certificates to config maps in namespaces.\nfunc (s *Server) shouldStartNsController() bool {\n\tif s.isK8SSigning() {\n\t\t// Need to distribute the roots from MeshConfig\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tif s.CA == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// For no CA we don't distribute it either, as there is no cert\n\tif features.PilotCertProvider == constants.CertProviderNone {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// StartCA starts the CA or RA server if configured.\nfunc (s *Server) startCA(caOpts *caOptions) {\n\tif s.CA == nil && s.RA == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\t// init the RA server if configured, else start init CA server\n\tif s.RA != nil {\n\t\tlog.Infof(\"initializing CA server with RA\")\n\t\ts.initCAServer(s.RA, caOpts)\n\t} else if s.CA != nil {\n\t\tlog.Infof(\"initializing
